This applies not only to everyday life but also to the financial markets.\n\nThe most substantial asset booms have historically followed wars, particularly after World War I and World War II. History has demonstrated this undeniable fact. The most crucial aspect is to have a well-defined strategy, manage risk intelligently, and continuously gain insights into the market. We are on the brink of weathering storms and surging waves in the near future.
